	  &lt;!-- Database node port number --&gt;
      &lt;PARAM name="dataPortBase" value="15400"/&gt;
	  &lt;!-- Data directory on the primary database node and data directories of standby nodes --&gt;
      &lt;PARAM name="dataNode1" value="/opt/huawei/install/data/dn,node2_hostname,/opt/huawei/install/data/dn"/&gt;
	  &lt;!-- Number of nodes for which the synchronization mode is set on the database node --&gt;
      &lt;PARAM name="dataNode1_syncNum" value="0"/&gt;
    &lt;/DEVICE&gt;
  &lt;!-- Information about the node deployment on node2 --&gt;
    &lt;DEVICE sn="node2_hostname"&gt;
	  &lt;!-- Host name of node2 --&gt;
      &lt;PARAM name="name" value="node2_hostname"/&gt;
	  &lt;!-- AZ where node1 is located and AZ priority --&gt;
      &lt;PARAM name="azName" value="AZ1"/&gt;
      &lt;PARAM name="azPriority" value="1"/&gt;
	  &lt;!-- IP address of node1. If only one NIC is available for the server, set backIP1 and sshIP1 to the same IP address. --&gt;
      &lt;PARAM name="backIp1" value="192.168.0.2"/&gt;
      &lt;PARAM name="sshIp1" value="192.168.0.2"/&gt;
    &lt;/DEVICE&gt;
  &lt;/DEVICELIST&gt;
&lt;/ROOT&gt;
</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Initializing the Installation Environment</h3><a id="user-content-initializing-the-installation-environment" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Initializing the Installation Environment" href="#initializing-the-installation-environment"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">After the openGauss configuration file is created, you need to run the gs_preinstall script to prepare the account and environment so that you can perform openGauss installation and management operations with the minimum permission, ensuring system security.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Precautions</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>You must check the upper-layer directory permissions to ensure that the user has the read, write, and execution permissions on the installation package and configuration file directory.</li>
<li>The mapping between each host name and IP address in the XML configuration file must be correct.</li>
<li>Only user root is authorized to run the gs_preinstall command.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Procedure</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Log in to any host where the openGauss is to be installed as user root and create a directory for storing the installation package as planned.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="mkdir -p /opt/software/openGauss
chmod 755 -R /opt/software"><pre class="notranslate"><code>mkdir -p /opt/software/openGauss
chmod 755 -R /opt/software
</code></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTE:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Do not create the directory in the home directory or subdirectory of any openGauss user because you may lack permissions for such directories.</li>
<li>The openGauss user must have the read and write permissions on the /opt/software/openGauss directory.</li>
</ul>
</blockquote>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">The release package is used as an example. Upload the installation package openGauss_x.x.x_PACKAGES_RELEASE.tar.gz and the configuration file clusterconfig.xml to the directory created in the previous step.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Go to the directory for storing the uploaded software package and decompress the package.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd /opt/software/openGauss
tar -zxvf openGauss_x.x.x_PACKAGES_RELEASE.tar.gz"><pre class="notranslate"><code>cd /opt/software/openGauss
tar -zxvf openGauss_x.x.x_PACKAGES_RELEASE.tar.gz
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Decompress the openGauss-x.x.x-openEULER-64bit.tar.gz package.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="tar -zxvf openGauss-x.x.x-openEULER-64bit.tar.gz"><pre class="notranslate"><code>tar -zxvf openGauss-x.x.x-openEULER-64bit.tar.gz
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">After the installation package is decompressed, the script subdirectory is automatically generated in /opt/software/openGauss. OM tool scripts such as gs_preinstall are generated in the script subdirectory.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Go to the directory for storing tool scripts.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd /opt/software/openGauss/script"><pre class="notranslate"><code>cd /opt/software/openGauss/script
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">To ensure that the OpenSSL version is correct, load the lib library in the installation package before preinstallation. Run the following command. {packagePath} indicates the path where the installation package is stored. In this example, the path is /opt/software/openGauss.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export LD_LIBRARY_PATH={packagePath}/script/gspylib/clib:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH"><pre class="notranslate"><code>export LD_LIBRARY_PATH={packagePath}/script/gspylib/clib:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">To ensure successful installation, check whether the values of hostname and /etc/hostname are the same. During preinstallation, the host name is checked.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Execute gs_preinstall to configure the installation environment. If the shared environment is used, add the --sep-env-file=ENVFILE parameter to separate environment variables to avoid mutual impact with other users. The environment variable separation file path is specified by users.
Execute gs_preinstall in interactive mode. During the execution, the mutual trust between users root and between clusteropenGauss users is automatically established.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./gs_preinstall -U omm -G dbgrp -X /opt/software/ openGauss/clusterconfig.xml"><pre class="notranslate"><code>./gs_preinstall -U omm -G dbgrp -X /opt/software/ openGauss/clusterconfig.xml
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">omm is the database administrator (also the OS user running the openGauss), dbgrp is the group name of the OS user running the openGauss, and /opt/software/ openGauss/clusterconfig.xml is the path of the openGauss configuration file. During the execution, you need to determine whether to establish mutual trust as prompted and enter the password of user root or the openGauss user.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Executing Installation</h3><a id="user-content-executing-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Executing Installation" href="#executing-installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">After the openGauss installation environment is prepared by executing the pre-installation script, deploy openGauss based on the installation process.
<strong>Prerequisites</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>You have successfully executed the gs_preinstall script.</li>
<li>All the server OSs and networks are functioning properly.</li>
<li>You have checked that the locale parameter for each server is set to the same value.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Procedure</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">(Optional) Check whether the installation package and openGauss configuration file exist in the planned directories. If no such package or file exists, perform the preinstallation again..</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Log in to any host of the openGauss and switch to the omm user.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="su - omm"><pre class="notranslate"><code>su - omm
</code></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTE:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>omm indicates the user specified by the -U parameter in the gs_preinstall script.</li>
<li>You need to execute the gs_install script as user omm specified in the gs_preinstall script. Otherwise, an execution error will be reported.</li>
</ul>
</blockquote>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Use gs_install to install the openGauss. If the openGauss is installed in environment variable separation mode, run the source command to obtain the environment variable separation file ENVFILE.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="gs_install -X /opt/software/ openGauss/clusterconfig.xml"><pre class="notranslate"><code>gs_install -X /opt/software/ openGauss/clusterconfig.xml
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The password must meet the following complexity requirements:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Contain at least eight characters.</li>
<li>Cannot be the same as the username, the current password (ALTER), or the current password in an inverted sequence.</li>
<li>Contain at least three of the following: uppercase characters (A to Z), lowercase characters (a to z), digits (0 to 9), and other characters (limited to ~!@#$%^&amp;*()-_=+|[{}];:,&lt;.&gt;/?).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">After the installation is successful, manually delete the trust between users root on the host, that is, delete the mutual trust file on each openGauss database node.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="rm –rf ~/.ssh"><pre class="notranslate"><code>rm –rf ~/.ssh
</code></pre></div>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Uninstalling the openGauss</h3><a id="user-content-uninstalling-the-opengauss" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Uninstalling the openGauss" href="#uninstalling-the-opengauss"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The process of uninstalling the openGauss includes uninstalling the openGauss and clearing the environment of the openGauss server.↵</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Executing Uninstallation</strong></h5><a id="user-content-executing-uninstallation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Executing Uninstallation" href="#executing-uninstallation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The openGauss provides an uninstallation script to help users uninstall the openGauss.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Procedure</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Log in as the OS user omm to the host where the CN is located.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Execute the gs_uninstall script to uninstall the database cluster.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="gs_uninstall --delete-data"><pre class="notranslate"><code>gs_uninstall --delete-data
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Alternatively, execute uninstallation on each openGauss node.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="gs_uninstall --delete-data -L"><pre class="notranslate"><code>gs_uninstall --delete-data -L
</code></pre></div>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto"><strong>Deleting openGauss Configurations</strong></h5><a id="user-content-deleting-opengauss-configurations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Deleting openGauss Configurations" href="#deleting-opengauss-configurations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">After the openGauss is uninstalled, execute the gs_postuninstall script to delete configurations from all servers in the openGauss if you do not need to re-deploy the openGauss using these configurations. These configurations are made by the gs_preinstall script.
<strong>Prerequisites</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The openGauss uninstallation task has been successfully executed.</li>
<li>User root is trustworthy and available.</li>
<li>Only user root is authorized to run the gs_postuninstall command.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Procedure</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Log in to the openGauss server as user root.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Run the ssh Host name command to check whether mutual trust has been successfully established. Then, enter exit.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="plat1:~ # ssh plat2 
Last login: Tue Jan  5 10:28:18 2016 from plat1 
plat2:~ # exit 
logout 
Connection to plat2 closed. 
plat1:~ #"><pre class="notranslate"><code>plat1:~ # ssh plat2 
Last login: Tue Jan  5 10:28:18 2016 from plat1 
plat2:~ # exit 
logout 
Connection to plat2 closed. 
plat1:~ #
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Go to the following path:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cd /opt/software/openGauss/script"><pre class="notranslate"><code>cd /opt/software/openGauss/script
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Run the gs_postuninstall command to clear the environment. If the openGauss is installed in environment variable separation mode, run the source command to obtain the environment variable separation file ENVFILE.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./gs_postuninstall -U omm -X /opt/software/openGauss/clusterconfig.xml --delete-user --delete-group"><pre class="notranslate"><code>./gs_postuninstall -U omm -X /opt/software/openGauss/clusterconfig.xml --delete-user --delete-group
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Alternatively, locally use the gs_postuninstall tool to clear each openGauss node.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./gs_postuninstall -U omm -X /opt/software/openGauss/clusterconfig.xml --delete-user --delete-group -L"><pre class="notranslate"><code>./gs_postuninstall -U omm -X /opt/software/openGauss/clusterconfig.xml --delete-user --delete-group -L
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">omm is the name of the OS user who runs the openGauss, and the path of the openGauss configuration file is /opt/software/openGauss/clusterconfig.xml.
If the cluster is installed in environment variable separation mode, delete the environment variable separation parameter ENV obtained by running the source command.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="unset MPPDB_ENV_SEPARATE_PATH"><pre class="notranslate"><code>unset MPPDB_ENV_SEPARATE_PATH
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Delete the mutual trust between the users root on each openGauss database node.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Compilation</h2><a id="user-content-compilation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Compilation" href="#compilation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Overview</h3><a id="user-content-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Overview" href="#overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To compile openGauss, you need two components: openGauss-server and binarylibs.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">openGauss-server: main code of openGauss. You can obtain it from the open source community.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">binarylibs: third party open source software that openGauss depends on. You can obtain it by compiling the openGauss-third_party code or downloading from the open source community on which we have compiled a copy and uploaded it . The first method will be introduced in the following chapter.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Before you compile openGauss，please check the OS and software dependency requirements.</p>
<p dir="auto">You can compile openGauss by build.sh, a one-click shell tool, which we will introduce later, or compile by command. Also, an installation package is produced by build.sh.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">OS and Software Dependency Requirements</h3><a id="user-content-os-and-software-dependency-requirements" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: OS and Software Dependency Requirements" href="#os-and-software-dependency-requirements"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The following OSs are supported:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">CentOS 7.6 (x86 architecture)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">openEuler-20.03-LTS (aarch64 architecture)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">The following table lists the software requirements for compiling the openGauss.</p>
<p dir="auto">You are advised to use the default installation packages of the following dependent software in the listed OS installation CD-ROMs or sources. If the following software does not exist, refer to the recommended versions of the software.</p>
<p dir="auto">Software dependency requirements are as follows:</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Software</th>
<th>Recommended Version</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>libaio-devel</td>
<td>0.3.109-13</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>flex</td>
<td>2.5.31 or later</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>bison</td>
<td>2.7-4</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ncurses-devel</td>
<td>5.9-13.20130511</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>glibc-devel</td>
<td>2.17-111</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>patch</td>
<td>2.7.1-10</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>lsb_release</td>
<td>4.1</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Downloading openGauss</h3><a id="user-content-downloading-opengauss" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Downloading openGauss" href="#downloading-opengauss"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can download openGauss-server and openGauss-third_party from open source community.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://opengauss.org/zh/" rel="nofollow">https://opengauss.org/zh/</a></p>
<p dir="auto">From the following website, you can obtain the binarylibs we have compiled. Please unzip it and rename to <strong>binarylibs</strong> after you download.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://opengauss.obs.cn-south-1.myhuaweicloud.com/2.1.0/openGauss-third_party_binarylibs.tar.gz" rel="nofollow">https://opengauss.obs.cn-south-1.myhuaweicloud.com/2.1.0/openGauss-third_party_binarylibs.tar.gz</a></p>
<p dir="auto">Now we have completed openGauss code, for example, we store it in following directories.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>/sda/openGauss-server</li>
<li>/sda/binarylibs</li>
<li>/sda/openGauss-third_party</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Compiling Third-Party Software</h3><a id="user-content-compiling-third-party-software" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Compiling Third-Party Software" href="#compiling-third-party-software"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Before compiling the openGauss, compile and build the open-source and third-party software on which the openGauss depends. These open-source and third-party software is stored in the openGauss-third_party code repository and usually needs to be built only once. If the open-source software is updated, rebuild the software.</p>
<p dir="auto">You can also directly obtain the output file of the open-source software compilation and build from the <strong>binarylibs</strong> repository.</p>
<p dir="auto">If you want to compile third-party by yourself, please go to openGauss-third_party repository to see details.</p>
<p dir="auto">After the preceding script is executed, the final compilation and build result is stored in the <strong>binarylibs</strong> directory at the same level as <strong>openGauss-third_party</strong>. These files will be used during the compilation of <strong>openGauss-server</strong>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Compiling by build.sh</h3><a id="user-content-compiling-by-buildsh" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Compiling by build.sh" href="#compiling-by-buildsh"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">build.sh in openGauss-server is an important script tool during compilation. It integrates software installation and compilation and product installation package compilation functions to quickly compile and package code.</p>
<p dir="auto">The following table describes the parameters.</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">Option</th>
<th align="left">Default Value</th>
<th align="left">Parameter</th>
<th align="left">Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left">-h</td>
<td align="left">Do not use this option.</td>
<td align="left">-</td>
<td align="left">Help menu.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">-m</td>
<td align="left">release</td>
<td align="left">[debug | release | memcheck]</td>
<td align="left">Selects the target version.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">-3rd</td>
<td align="left">${Code directory}/binarylibs</td>
<td align="left">[binarylibs path]</td>
<td align="left">Specifies the path of binarylibs. The path must be an absolute path.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">-pkg</td>
<td align="left">Do not use this option.</td>
<td align="left">-</td>
<td align="left">Compresses the code compilation result into an installation package.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTICE:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>-m [debug | release | memcheck]</strong> indicates that three target versions can be selected:
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>release</strong>: indicates that the binary program of the release version is generated. During compilation of this version, the GCC high-level optimization option is configured to remove the kernel debugging code. This option is usually used in the generation environment or performance test environment.</li>
<li><strong>debug</strong>: indicates that a binary program of the debug version is generated. During compilation of this version, the kernel code debugging function is added, which is usually used in the development self-test environment.</li>
<li><strong>memcheck</strong>: indicates that a binary program of the memcheck version is generated. During compilation of this version, the ASAN function is added based on the debug version to locate memory problems.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>-3rd [binarylibs path]</strong> is the path of <strong>binarylibs</strong>. By default, <strong>binarylibs</strong> exists in the current code folder. If <strong>binarylibs</strong> is moved to <strong>openGauss-server</strong> or a soft link to <strong>binarylibs</strong> is created in <strong>openGauss-server</strong>, you do not need to specify the parameter. However, if you do so, please note that the file is easy to be deleted by the <strong>git clean</strong> command.</li>
<li>Each option in this script has a default value. The number of options is small and the dependency is simple. Therefore, this script is easy to use. If the required value is different from the default value, set this parameter based on the actual requirements.</li>
</ol>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Now you know the usage of build.sh, so you can compile the openGauss-server by one command with build.sh.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m [debug | release | memcheck] -3rd [binarylibs path]"><pre class="notranslate"><code>[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m [debug | release | memcheck] -3rd [binarylibs path]
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">For example:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh       # Compile openGauss of the release version. The binarylibs or its soft link must exist in the code directory. Otherwise, the operation fails.
[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m debug -3rd /sda/binarylibs    # Compilate openGauss of the debug version using binarylibs we put on /sda/"><pre class="notranslate"><code>[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh       # Compile openGauss of the release version. The binarylibs or its soft link must exist in the code directory. Otherwise, the operation fails.
[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m debug -3rd /sda/binarylibs    # Compilate openGauss of the debug version using binarylibs we put on /sda/
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The software installation path after compilation is <strong>/sda/openGauss-server/dest</strong>.</p>
<p dir="auto">The compiled binary files are stored in <strong>/sda/openGauss-server/dest/bin</strong>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Compilation log: <strong>make_compile.log</strong></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Compiling by Command</h3><a id="user-content-compiling-by-command" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Compiling by Command" href="#compiling-by-command"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Run the following script to obtain the system version:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh src/get_PlatForm_str.sh"><pre class="notranslate"><code>[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh src/get_PlatForm_str.sh
</code></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTICE:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The command output indicates the OSs supported by the openGauss. The OSs supported by the openGauss are centos7.6_x86_64 and openeuler_aarch64.</li>
<li>If <strong>Failed</strong> or another version is displayed, the openGauss does not support the current operating system.</li>
</ul>
</blockquote>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Configure environment variables, add <strong>____</strong> based on the code download location, and replace *** with the result obtained in the previous step.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export CODE_BASE=________     # Path of the openGauss-server file
export BINARYLIBS=________    # Path of the binarylibs file
export GAUSSHOME=$CODE_BASE/dest/
export GCC_PATH=$BINARYLIBS/buildtools/***/gcc7.3/
export CC=$GCC_PATH/gcc/bin/gccexport CXX=$GCC_PATH/gcc/bin/g++
export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$GAUSSHOME/lib:$GCC_PATH/gcc/lib64:$GCC_PATH/isl/lib:$GCC_PATH/mpc/lib/:$GCC_PATH/mpfr/lib/:$GCC_PATH/gmp/lib/:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
export PATH=$GAUSSHOME/bin:$GCC_PATH/gcc/bin:$PATH
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>export CODE_BASE=________     # Path of the openGauss-server file
export BINARYLIBS=________    # Path of the binarylibs file
export GAUSSHOME=$CODE_BASE/dest/
export GCC_PATH=$BINARYLIBS/buildtools/***/gcc7.3/
export CC=$GCC_PATH/gcc/bin/gccexport CXX=$GCC_PATH/gcc/bin/g++
export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$GAUSSHOME/lib:$GCC_PATH/gcc/lib64:$GCC_PATH/isl/lib:$GCC_PATH/mpc/lib/:$GCC_PATH/mpfr/lib/:$GCC_PATH/gmp/lib/:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
export PATH=$GAUSSHOME/bin:$GCC_PATH/gcc/bin:$PATH

</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Select a version and configure it.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>debug</strong> version:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./configure --gcc-version=7.3.0 CC=g++ CFLAGS='-O0' --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-debug --enable-cassert --enable-thread-safety --without-readline --without-zlib"><pre class="notranslate"><code>./configure --gcc-version=7.3.0 CC=g++ CFLAGS='-O0' --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-debug --enable-cassert --enable-thread-safety --without-readline --without-zlib
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>release</strong> version:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./configure --gcc-version=7.3.0 CC=g++ CFLAGS=&quot;-O2 -g3&quot; --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-thread-safety --without-readline --without-zlib"><pre class="notranslate"><code>./configure --gcc-version=7.3.0 CC=g++ CFLAGS="-O2 -g3" --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-thread-safety --without-readline --without-zlib
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>memcheck</strong> version:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./configure --gcc-version=7.3.0 CC=g++ CFLAGS='-O0' --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-debug --enable-cassert --enable-thread-safety --without-readline --without-zlib --enable-memory-check"><pre class="notranslate"><code>./configure --gcc-version=7.3.0 CC=g++ CFLAGS='-O0' --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-debug --enable-cassert --enable-thread-safety --without-readline --without-zlib --enable-memory-check
</code></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>NOTICE:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><em>[debug | release | memcheck]</em> indicates that three target versions are available.</li>
<li>On the ARM-based platform, <strong>-D__USE_NUMA</strong> needs to be added to <strong>CFLAGS</strong>.</li>
<li>On the <strong>ARMv8.1</strong> platform or a later version (for example, Kunpeng 920), <strong>-D__ARM_LSE</strong> needs to be added to <strong>CFLAGS</strong>.</li>
<li>If <strong>binarylibs</strong> is moved to <strong>openGauss-server</strong> or a soft link to <strong>binarylibs</strong> is created in <strong>openGauss-server</strong>, you do not need to specify the <strong>--3rd</strong> parameter. However, if you do so, please note that the file is easy to be deleted by the <code>git clean</code> command.</li>
<li>To build with mysql_fdw, add <strong>--enable-mysql-fdw</strong> when configure. Note that before build mysql_fdw, MariaDB's C client library is needed.</li>
<li>To build with oracle_fdw, add <strong>--enable-oracle-fdw</strong> when configure. Note that before build oracle_fdw, Oracle's C client library is needed.</li>
</ol>
</blockquote>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Run the following commands to compile openGauss:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[user@linux openGauss-server]$ make -sj
[user@linux openGauss-server]$ make install -sj"><pre class="notranslate"><code>[user@linux openGauss-server]$ make -sj
[user@linux openGauss-server]$ make install -sj
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">If the following information is displayed, the compilation and installation are successful:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="openGauss installation complete."><pre class="notranslate"><code>openGauss installation complete.
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The software installation path after compilation is <strong>$GAUSSHOME</strong>.</p>
<p dir="auto">The compiled binary files are stored in <strong>$GAUSSHOME/bin</strong>.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Compiling the Installation Package</h3><a id="user-content-compiling-the-installation-package" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Compiling the Installation Package" href="#compiling-the-installation-package"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Please read the chapter <strong>Compiling by build.sh</strong> first to understand the usage of build.sh and how to compile openGauss by using the script.</p>
<p dir="auto">Now you can compile the installation package with just adding a option <code>-pkg</code>.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m [debug | release | memcheck] -3rd [binarylibs path] -pkg"><pre class="notranslate"><code>[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m [debug | release | memcheck] -3rd [binarylibs path] -pkg
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">For example:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -pkg      # Compile openGauss installation package of the release version. The binarylibs or its soft link must exist in the code directory. Otherwise, the operation fails.
[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m debug -3rd /sda/binarylibs -pkg   # Compile openGauss installation package of the debug version using binarylibs we put on /sda/"><pre class="notranslate"><code>[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -pkg      # Compile openGauss installation package of the release version. The binarylibs or its soft link must exist in the code directory. Otherwise, the operation fails.
[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m debug -3rd /sda/binarylibs -pkg   # Compile openGauss installation package of the debug version using binarylibs we put on /sda/
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The generated installation package is stored in the <strong>./package</strong> directory.</p>
<p dir="auto">Compilation log: <strong>make_compile.log</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Installation package packaging log: <strong>./package/make_package.log</strong></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quick Start</h2><a id="user-content-quick-start" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quick Start" href="#quick-start"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">See the <a href="https://opengauss.org/zh/docs/2.1.0/docs/Quickstart/Quickstart.html" rel="nofollow">Quick Start</a> to implement the image classification.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Docs</h2><a id="user-content-docs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Docs" href="#docs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">For more details about the installation guide, tutorials, and APIs, please see the <a href="https://gitee.com/opengauss/docs" rel="nofollow">User Documentation</a>.</p>

    <div id="js-global-screen-reader-notice-assertive" class="sr-only mt-n1" aria-live="assertive" aria-atomic="true"></div>
  </body>
</html>
